SELECT (s1.ra-s2.ra)*3600.0*COS(RADIANS(s1.dec)) as deltaRA, (s1.dec-s2.dec)*3600.0 as deltaDec, (s1.uAperMag3-s2.uAperMag3) as dy, (s1.gAperMag3-s2.gAperMag3) as dj1, (s1.rAperMag3-s2.rAperMag3) as dh, (s1.iAperMag3-s2.iAperMag3) as dk FROM atlasSource AS s1, atlasSource AS s2, atlasSourceNeighbours AS x WHERE s1.uAperMag3 > 0 AND s2.uAperMag3 > 0 AND s1.gAperMag3 > 0 AND s2.gAperMag3 > 0 AND s1.rAperMag3 > 0 AND s2.rAperMag3 > 0 AND s1.iAperMag3 > 0 AND s2.iAperMag3 > 0 AND masterObjID=s1.sourceID AND slaveObjID=s2.sourceID AND s1.priOrSec=s1.frameSetID AND distanceMins<0.01 AND distanceMins IN ( SELECT MIN(distanceMins) FROM atlasSourceNeighbours WHERE masterObjID=x.masterObjID)

select top 10 * from bestdr9..photoobj /*ramses5..*/

as petromag_z, /*21*/ dr9.petromagerr_u as petromagerr_u , /*22*/ dr9.petromagerr_g as petromagerr_g , /*23*/ dr9.petromagerr_r as petromagerr_r , /*24*/ dr9.petromagerr_i as petromagerr_i , /*25*/ isdssextinction, /*30*/ dr9.extinction_z as zsdssextinction, /*31*/ dr9.objID as dr9ID, /*32*/ X.distancemins as separation, /*33*/ X.masterobjID as MasterID, /*34*/ X.slaveobjID as slaveID, /*35*/ photoz.z as PhotoZ, /*36*/ photoz.zerr as PhotoZErr, /*37*/ spec.z as specZ From atlassource as atlas, atlassourcexdr9photoobj as X, bestdr9..photoobj as dr9, bestdr9..photozrf as photoz, Select atlas.upetromag as upetromag, atlas.gpetromag as gpetromag, atlas.rpetromag as rpetromag, atlas.ipetromag as ipetromag, atlas.zpetromag as zpetromag, atlas.au as uatlasextinction , atlas.ag as gatlasextinction , atlas.ar as ratlasextinction, atlas.ai as iatlasextinction, atlas.az as zatlasextinction, photoobj.petromag_u , photoobj.petromag_g , photoobj.petromag_r , photoobj.petromag_i , photoobj.petromag_z , photoobj.extinction_u, photoobj.extinction_g, photoobj.extinction_r, photoobj.extinction_i, photoobj.extinction_z, photozrf.z, atlas.ra as ATLAS_RA , atlas.dec as ATLAS_DEC , photoobj.ra as PHOTOOBJ_RA , photoobj.dec as PHOTOOBJ_DEC , atlas.sourceId as ATLAS_ID , photoobj.objID as SDSS_ID FROM atlassource as atlas, bestdr9..photoobj as photoobj, bestdr9..photozrf as photozrf, atlassourcexdr9photoobj as X WHERE X.masterobjID = atlas.sourceID AND photozrf.objid = photoobj.objid AND photozrf.objid = X.slaveobjid AND atlas.gpetromag >0 and atlas.rpetromag >0 and atlas.ipetromag >0 and atlas.zpetromag >0 AND X.distanceMins < 1/60.0  
Select atlas.upetromag as upetromag, atlas.gpetromag as gpetromag, atlas.rpetromag as rpetromag, atlas.ipetromag as ipetromag, atlas.zpetromag as zpetromag, atlas.au as uatlasextinction , atlas.ag as gatlasextinction , atlas.ar as ratlasextinction, atlas.ai as iatlasextinction, atlas.az as zatlasextinction, photoobj.petromag_u , photoobj.petromag_g , photoobj.petromag_r , photoobj.petromag_i , photoobj.petromag_z , photoobj.extinction_u, photoobj.extinction_g, photoobj.extinction_r, photoobj.extinction_i, photoobj.extinction_z, photozrf.z, spec.z as specZ FROM atlassource as atlas, bestdr9..photoobj as photoobj, bestdr9..photozrf as photozrf, atlassourcexdr9photoobj as X, bestdr9..specobjall as spec WHERE X.masterobjID = atlas.sourceID AND photozrf.objid = photoobj.objid AND photozrf.objid = X.slaveobjid AND photozrf.objid = spec.bestobjid AND atlas.gpetromag >0 and atlas.rpetromag >0 and atlas.ipetromag >0 and atlas.zpetromag >0 AND X.distanceMins < 1/60.0 AND spec.z >0

uatlasextinction , atlas.ag as gatlasextinction , atlas.ar as ratlasextinction, atlas.ai as iatlasextinction, atlas.az as zatlasextinction, dr9.petromag_u as petromag_u, dr9.petromag_g as petromag_g, dr9.petromag_r as petromag_r, dr9.petromag_i as petromag_i, dr9.petromag_z as petromag_z, dr9.petromagerr_u as petromagerr_u , dr9.petromagerr_g as petromagerr_g , dr9.petromagerr_r as petromagerr_r , SELECT (s1.ra-s2.ra)*3600.0*COS(RADIANS(s1.dec)) as deltaRA, (s1.dec-s2.dec)*3600.0 as deltaDec, (s1.uAperMag3-s2.uAperMag3) as du, (s1.gAperMag3-s2.gAperMag3) as dg, (s1.rAperMag3-s2.rAperMag3) as dr, (s1.iAperMag3-s2.iAperMag3) as di FROM atlasSource AS s1, atlasSource AS s2, atlasSourceNeighbours AS x WHERE s1.uAperMag3 > 0 AND s2.uAperMag3 > 0 AND s1.gAperMag3 > 0 AND s2.gAperMag3 > 0 AND s1.rAperMag3 > 0 AND s2.rAperMag3 > 0 AND s1.iAperMag3 > 0 AND s2.iAperMag3 > 0 AND masterObjID=s1.sourceID AND slaveObjID=s2.sourceID AND s1.priOrSec=s1.frameSetID AND distanceMins<0.01 AND distanceMins IN ( SELECT MIN(distanceMins) FROM atlasSourceNeighbours WHERE masterObjID=x.masterObjID)
